\hypertarget{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga1bcb3f29f3cfbe896517e7bb6ebeaf03}{\index{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}!Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock}}
\index{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock}!CHIP: LPC17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}}
\subsubsection[{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-Periph\-Clock (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-H\-I\-P\-\_\-\-S\-Y\-S\-C\-T\-L\-\_\-\-C\-L\-O\-C\-K\-\_\-\-T}}]{clk}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga1bcb3f29f3cfbe896517e7bb6ebeaf03}


Disables power and clocking for a peripheral. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clk} & Clock to disable \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only peripheral clocks that are defined in the P\-C\-O\-N\-P registers of the clock and power controller can be enabled and disabled with this function. Some clocks need to be disabled elsewhere (ie, U\-S\-B) and will return false to indicate it can't be disabled with this function. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga3b9589b6a14d39653503be3693990f8f}{\index{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}!Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L}}
\index{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L}!CHIP: LPC17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}}
\subsubsection[{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Disable\-P\-L\-L (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-H\-I\-P\-\_\-\-S\-Y\-S\-C\-T\-L\-\_\-\-P\-L\-L\-\_\-\-T}}]{P\-L\-L\-Num, }
\item[{uint32\-\_\-t}]{flags}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga3b9589b6a14d39653503be3693990f8f}


Disables or disconnects a P\-L\-L. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em P\-L\-L\-Num} & P\-L\-L number \\
\hline
{\em flags} & S\-Y\-S\-C\-T\-L\-\_\-\-P\-L\-L\-\_\-\-E\-N\-A\-B\-L\-E or S\-Y\-S\-C\-T\-L\-\_\-\-P\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-N\-N\-E\-C\-T \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This will also perform a P\-L\-L feed sequence. Connect only applies to the L\-P\-C175x/6x devices.

Enables power and clocking for a peripheral. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clk} & Clock to enable \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Only peripheral clocks that are defined in the P\-C\-O\-N\-P registers of the clock and power controller can be enabled and disabled with this function. Some clocks need to be enabled elsewhere (ie, U\-S\-B) and will return false to indicate it can't be enabled with this function. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Gets the C\-P\-U clock divider. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
C\-P\-U clock divider, between 1 and divider max 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The maximum divider for the 175x/6x is 256. The maximum divider for the 177x/8x and 407x/8x is 32. Note on 175x/6x devices, the divided C\-P\-U clock rate is used as the input to the peripheral clock dividers, while 177x/8x and 407x/8x devices use the undivided C\-P\-U clock rate. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Gets a clock divider for a peripheral. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clk} & Clock to set divider for \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The divider for the clock 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Selects the divider for a peripheral. A peripheral clock is generated from the C\-P\-U clock divided by its peripheral clock divider. Only peripheral clocks that are defined in the P\-C\-L\-K\-S\-E\-L registers of the clock and power controller can used this function. (L\-P\-C175\-X/6\-X only) 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga9c2bc86c857119426aa6a724c12a6f42}{\index{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}!Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate}}
\index{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate}!CHIP: LPC17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}}
\subsubsection[{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\-\_\-t Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Get\-Peripheral\-Clock\-Rate (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf C\-H\-I\-P\-\_\-\-S\-Y\-S\-C\-T\-L\-\_\-\-P\-C\-L\-K\-\_\-\-T}}]{clk}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_ga9c2bc86c857119426aa6a724c12a6f42}


Returns clock rate for a peripheral (from peripheral clock) 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clk} & Clock to get rate of \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Clock rate for the peripheral 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This covers most common peripheral clocks, but not every clock in the system. L\-P\-C177x/8x and L\-P\-C407x/8x devices use the same clock for all periphreals, while the L\-P\-C175x/6x have unique dividers (except to R\-T\-C ) that may alter the peripheral clock rate. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Selects a source clock and divider rate for the C\-L\-K\-O\-U\-T pin. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em src} & source selected \\
\hline
{\em div} & Divider for the clock source on C\-L\-K\-O\-U\-T, 1 to 16 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function will disable the C\-L\-K\-O\-U\-T signal if its enabled. Use Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Enable\-C\-L\-K\-O\-U\-T to re-\/enable C\-L\-K\-O\-U\-T after a call to this function. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_gaf88a9722800b98c3ea3cccb572c54230}{\index{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}!Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div}}
\index{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div}!CHIP: LPC17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}}
\subsubsection[{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Set\-C\-P\-U\-Clock\-Div (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{uint32\-\_\-t}]{div}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_gaf88a9722800b98c3ea3cccb572c54230}


Sets the C\-P\-U clock divider. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em div} & C\-P\-U clock divider, between 1 and divider max \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The maximum divider for the 175x/6x is 256. The maximum divider for the 177x/8x and 407x/8x is 32. Note on 175x/6x devices, the divided C\-P\-U clock rate is used as the input to the peripheral clock dividers, while 177x/8x and 407x/8x devices use the undivided C\-P\-U clock rate. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_gab218e9b1ee5377bd662e516420e863ea}


Selects a clock divider for a peripheral. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clk} & Clock to set divider for \\
\hline
{\em div} & Divider for the clock \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Selects the divider for a peripheral. A peripheral clock is generated from the C\-P\-U clock divided by its peripheral clock divider. Only peripheral clocks that are defined in the P\-C\-L\-K\-S\-E\-L registers of the clock and power controller can used this function. (L\-P\-C175\-X/6\-X only) 
\end{DoxyNote}
\hypertarget{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_gaf4a2dd4c6aae5d6b830f7cf529ec8773}{\index{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver@{C\-H\-I\-P\-: L\-P\-C17xx/40xx Clock Driver}!Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Setup\-P\-L\-L@{Chip\-\_\-\-Clock\-\_\-\-Setup\-P\-L\-L}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{group__CLOCK__17XX__40XX_gaf4a2dd4c6aae5d6b830f7cf529ec8773}


Sets up a P\-L\-L. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em P\-L\-L\-Num} & P\-L\-L number \\
\hline
{\em msel} & P\-L\-L Multiplier value (Must be pre-\/decremented) \\
\hline
{\em psel} & P\-L\-L Divider value (Must be pre-\/decremented) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
See the User Manual for limitations on these values for stable P\-L\-L operation. Be careful with these values -\/ they must be safe values for the msl, nsel, and psel registers so must be already decremented by 1 or the the correct value for psel (0 = div by 1, 1 = div by 2, etc.). 
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Nothing 
\end{DoxyReturn}
